<h2 id="anatomy" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Anatomy</h2>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.Label</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.Content</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.ItemGroup</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.ItemGroupLabel</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.Item</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.ItemText</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.ItemIndicator</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.Item</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.ItemGroup</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.Content</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.ValueText</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<h3 id="basic" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#basic"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Basic</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Here&#x27;s a basic example of the Listbox component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8dhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8dhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8dhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The Listbox component can be controlled by using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> props. This allows you to manage the
selected value externally.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8jhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8jhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8jhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the listbox is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useListbox</code> hook. This way you
can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="disabled-item" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#disabled-item"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Disabled Item</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Listbox items can be disabled using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">disabled</code> prop on the collection item.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can also use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">isItemDisabled</code> within the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">createListCollection</code> to disable items based on a condition.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 id="multiple" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#multiple"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Multiple</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">selectionMode</code> property as <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">multiple</code> to allow the user to select multiple items at a time.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_97hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_97hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_97hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="grouping" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#grouping"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Grouping</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The Listbox component supports grouping items. You can use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">groupBy</code> function to group items based on a specific
property.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="extended-selection" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#extended-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Extended Selection</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The extended selection mode allows users to select multiple items using keyboard modifiers like <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Cmd</code> (Mac) or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Ctrl</code>
(Windows/Linux).</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="horizontal" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#horizontal"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Horizontal</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">orientation</code> prop to display the listbox items horizontally.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="grid-layout" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#grid-layout"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Grid Layout</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">createGridCollection</code> to display items in a grid layout with keyboard navigation support.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="filtering" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#filtering"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Filtering</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useListCollection</code> with the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">filter</code> function to enable filtering of items.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a5hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a5hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a5hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="select-all" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#select-all"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Select All</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useListboxContext</code> to implement a &quot;Select All&quot; functionality that allows users to select or deselect all items at
once.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_abhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_abhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_abhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="value-text" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#value-text"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Value Text</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Listbox.ValueText</code> to display the selected values as a comma-separated string.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_ahhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_ahhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_ahhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="type-safety" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#type-safety"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Type Safety</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Listbox.RootComponent</code> type enables you to create typed wrapper components that maintain full type safety for
collection items.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> Listbox</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">:</span><span style="color:#FFA657"> ArkListbox</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">.</span><span style="color:#FFA657">RootComponent</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (</span><span style="color:#FFA657">props</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">ArkListbox.Root</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> {...</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">props</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">{</span><span style="color:#8B949E">/* ... */</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">ArkListbox.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the wrapper with full type inference on <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> and other callbacks:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> App</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> () </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> collection</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> createListCollection</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    initialItems: [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      { label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;React&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;react&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      { label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Vue&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;vue&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">      collection</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">collection</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">      onValueChange</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">e</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">        // e.items is typed as Array&lt;{ label: string, value: string }&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(e.items)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      }</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">      {</span><span style="color:#8B949E">/* ... */</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Listbox</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Prop</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm <h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">API</h3><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm c_colorPalette.default">empty</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code c_colorPalette.default">highlightedValue</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">string</code><p class="text">The value of the highlighted item</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">highlightedItem</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code Anatomy\n\n{/* \u003cAnatomy id=\"listbox\" /\u003e */}\n\n```tsx\n\u003cListbox.Root\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Label /\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003cListbox.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.ItemGroupLabel /\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Item\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemText /\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator /\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.ItemGroup\u003e\n  \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.ValueText /\u003e\n\u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n### Basic\n\nHere's a basic example of the Listbox component.\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/react/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'United States', value: 'us' },\n      { label: 'United Kingdom', value: 'uk' },\n      { label: 'Canada', value: 'ca' },\n      { label: 'Australia', value: 'au' },\n      { label: 'Germany', value: 'de' },\n      { label: 'France', value: 'fr' },\n      { label: 'Japan', value: 'jp' },\n    ],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cListbox.Root className={styles.Root} collection={collection}\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Country\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n        {collection.items.map((item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cListbox.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} item={item}\u003e\n            \u003cListbox.ItemText className={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n            \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/solid/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'United States', value: 'us' },\n      { label: 'United Kingdom', value: 'uk' },\n      { label: 'Canada', value: 'ca' },\n      { label: 'Australia', value: 'au' },\n      { label: 'Germany', value: 'de' },\n      { label: 'France', value: 'fr' },\n      { label: 'Japan', value: 'jp' },\n    ],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cListbox.Root class={styles.Root} collection={collection}\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Country\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={collection.items}\u003e\n          {(item) =\u003e (\n            \u003cListbox.Item class={styles.Item} item={item()}\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item().label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/vue/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nconst collection = createListCollection({\n  items: [\n    { label: 'United States', value: 'us' },\n    { label: 'United Kingdom', value: 'uk' },\n    { label: 'Canada', value: 'ca' },\n    { label: 'Australia', value: 'au' },\n    { label: 'Germany', value: 'de' },\n    { label: 'France', value: 'fr' },\n    { label: 'Japan', value: 'jp' },\n  ],\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :collection=\"collection\"\u003e\n    \u003cListbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eSelect Country\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cListbox.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Item v-for=\"item in collection.items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :item=\"item\"\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemText :class=\"styles.ItemText\"\u003e{{ item.label }}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/svelte/listbox'\n  import CheckIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/check'\n  import styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'United States', value: 'us' },\n      { label: 'United Kingdom', value: 'uk' },\n      { label: 'Canada', value: 'ca' },\n      { label: 'Australia', value: 'au' },\n      { label: 'Germany', value: 'de' },\n      { label: 'France', value: 'fr' },\n      { label: 'Japan', value: 'jp' },\n    ],\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cListbox.Root class={styles.Root} {collection}\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Country\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n    {#each collection.items as item (item.value)}\n      \u003cListbox.Item class={styles.Item} {item}\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n\u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nThe Listbox component can be controlled by using the `value` and `onValueChange` props. This allows you to manage the\nselected value externally.\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/react/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Small', value: 'sm' },\n      { label: 'Medium', value: 'md' },\n      { label: 'Large', value: 'lg' },\n      { label: 'Extra Large', value: 'xl' },\n    ],\n  })\n  const [value, setValue] = useState(['md'])\n\n  return (\n    \u003cListbox.Root\n      className={styles.Root}\n      collection={collection}\n      value={value}\n      onValueChange={(e) =\u003e setValue(e.value)}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Size\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n        {collection.items.map((item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cListbox.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} item={item}\u003e\n            \u003cListbox.ItemText className={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n            \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/solid/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Small', value: 'sm' },\n      { label: 'Medium', value: 'md' },\n      { label: 'Large', value: 'lg' },\n      { label: 'Extra Large', value: 'xl' },\n    ],\n  })\n  const [value, setValue] = createSignal(['md'])\n\n  return (\n    \u003cListbox.Root class={styles.Root} collection={collection} value={value()} onValueChange={(e) =\u003e setValue(e.value)}\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Size\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={collection.items}\u003e\n          {(item) =\u003e (\n            \u003cListbox.Item class={styles.Item} item={item()}\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item().label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/vue/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nconst collection = createListCollection({\n  items: [\n    { label: 'Small', value: 'sm' },\n    { label: 'Medium', value: 'md' },\n    { label: 'Large', value: 'lg' },\n    { label: 'Extra Large', value: 'xl' },\n  ],\n})\n\nconst value = ref(['md'])\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :collection=\"collection\" v-model=\"value\"\u003e\n    \u003cListbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eSelect Size\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cListbox.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Item v-for=\"item in collection.items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :item=\"item\"\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemText :class=\"styles.ItemText\"\u003e{{ item.label }}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/svelte/listbox'\n  import CheckIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/check'\n  import styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Small', value: 'sm' },\n      { label: 'Medium', value: 'md' },\n      { label: 'Large', value: 'lg' },\n      { label: 'Extra Large', value: 'xl' },\n    ],\n  })\n\n  let value = $state(['md'])\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cListbox.Root class={styles.Root} {collection} {value} onValueChange={(e) =\u003e (value = e.value)}\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Size\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n    {#each collection.items as item (item.value)}\n      \u003cListbox.Item class={styles.Item} {item}\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n\u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the listbox is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useListbox` hook. This way you\ncan access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection, useListbox } from '@ark-ui/react/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Low', value: 'low' },\n      { label: 'Medium', value: 'medium' },\n      { label: 'High', value: 'high' },\n      { label: 'Critical', value: 'critical' },\n    ],\n  })\n  const listbox = useListbox({ collection })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e listbox.setValue(['high'])}\u003e\n        Set to High\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={listbox}\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Priority\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          {collection.items.map((item) =\u003e (\n            \u003cListbox.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} item={item}\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemText className={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection, useListbox } from '@ark-ui/solid/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Low', value: 'low' },\n      { label: 'Medium', value: 'medium' },\n      { label: 'High', value: 'high' },\n      { label: 'Critical', value: 'critical' },\n    ],\n  })\n  const listbox = useListbox({ collection })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e listbox().setValue(['high'])}\u003e\n        Set to High\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={listbox}\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.Label {(item) =\u003e (\n              \u003cListbox.Item class={styles.Item} item={item()}\u003e\n                \u003cListbox.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item().label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n                \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                  \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n              \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/Index\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection, useListbox } from '@ark-ui/vue/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { computed } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nconst collection = createListCollection({\n  items: [\n    { label: 'Low', value: 'low' },\n    { label: 'Medium', value: 'medium' },\n    { label: 'High', value: 'high' },\n    { label: 'Critical', value: 'critical' },\n  ],\n})\n\nconst listboxValue = useListbox({ collection })\nconst listbox = computed(() =\u003e listboxValue.value)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"listbox.setValue(['high'])\"\u003eSet to :class=\"styles.Item\" :item=\"item\"\u003e\n          \u003cListbox.ItemText :class=\"styles.ItemText\"\u003e{{ item.label }}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n          \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Listbox, createListCollection, useListbox } \u003cListbox.Item class={styles.Item} {item}\u003e\n          \u003cListbox.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n          \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n            \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n      {/each}\n    \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Listbox.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Disabled Item\n\nListbox items can be disabled using the `disabled` prop on the collection item.\n\n**Example: disabled-item**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/react/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const DisabledItem = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Free', value: 'free' },\n      { label: 'Pro', value: 'pro' },\n      { label: 'Enterprise', value: 'enterprise', disabled: true },\n      { label: 'Custom', value: 'custom' },\n    ],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cListbox.Root className={styles.Root} collection={collection}\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Plan\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n        {collection.items.map((item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cListbox.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} item={item}\u003e\n            \u003cListbox.ItemText className={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n            \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/solid/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const DisabledItem = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Free', value: 'free' },\n      { label: 'Pro', value: 'pro' },\n      { label: 'Enterprise', value: 'enterprise', disabled: true },\n      { label: 'Custom', value: 'custom' },\n    ],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cListbox.Root class={styles.Root} collection={collection}\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Plan\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={collection.items}\u003e\n          {(item) =\u003e (\n            \u003cListbox.Item class={styles.Item} item={item()}\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item().label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/vue/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nconst collection = createListCollection({\n  items: [\n    { label: 'Free', value: 'free' },\n    { label: 'Pro', value: 'pro' },\n    { label: 'Enterprise', value: 'enterprise', disabled: true },\n    { label: 'Custom', value: 'custom' },\n  ],\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :collection=\"collection\"\u003e\n    \u003cListbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eSelect Plan\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cListbox.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Item v-for=\"item in collection.items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :item=\"item\"\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemText :class=\"styles.ItemText\"\u003e{{ item.label }}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/svelte/listbox'\n  import CheckIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/check'\n  import styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Free', value: 'free' },\n      { label: 'Pro', value: 'pro' },\n      { label: 'Enterprise', value: 'enterprise', disabled: true },\n      { label: 'Custom', value: 'custom' },\n    ],\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cListbox.Root class={styles.Root} {collection}\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Plan\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n    {#each collection.items as item (item.value)}\n      \u003cListbox.Item class={styles.Item} {item}\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n\u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n\u003e You can also use the `isItemDisabled` within the `createListCollection` to disable items based on a condition.\n\n### Multiple\n\nYou can set the `selectionMode` property as `multiple` to allow the user to select multiple items at a time.\n\n**Example: multiple**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/react/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Multiple = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Monday', value: 'mon' },\n      { label: 'Tuesday', value: 'tue' },\n      { label: 'Wednesday', value: 'wed' },\n      { label: 'Thursday', value: 'thu' },\n      { label: 'Friday', value: 'fri' },\n      { label: 'Saturday', value: 'sat' },\n      { label: 'Sunday', value: 'sun' },\n    ],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cListbox.Root className={styles.Root} collection={collection} selectionMode=\"multiple\"\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Days\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n        {collection.items.map((item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cListbox.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} item={item}\u003e\n            \u003cListbox.ItemText className={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n            \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n              \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/solid/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nexport const Multiple = () =\u003e {\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: 'Monday', value: 'mon' },\n      { label: 'Tuesday', value: 'tue' },\n      { label: 'Wednesday', value: 'wed' },\n      { label: 'Thursday', value: 'thu' },\n      { label: 'Friday', value: 'fri' },\n      { label: 'Saturday', value: 'sat' },\n      { label: 'Sunday', value: 'sun' },\n    ],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cListbox.Root class={styles.Root} collection={collection} selectionMode=\"multiple\"\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Days\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={collection.items}\u003e\n          {(item) =\u003e (\n            \u003cListbox.Item class={styles.Item} item={item()}\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{item().label}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n              \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/vue/listbox'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\nconst collection = createListCollection({\n  items: [\n    { label: 'Monday', value: 'mon' },\n    { label: 'Tuesday', value: 'tue' },\n    { label: 'Wednesday', value: 'wed' },\n    { label: 'Thursday', value: 'thu' },\n    { label: 'Friday', value: 'fri' },\n    { label: 'Saturday', value: 'sat' },\n    { label: 'Sunday', value: 'sun' },\n  ],\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :collection=\"collection\" selectionMode=\"multiple\"\u003e\n    \u003cListbox.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eSelect Days\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n    \u003cListbox.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n      \u003cListbox.Item v-for=\"item in collection.items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :item=\"item\"\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemText :class=\"styles.ItemText\"\u003e{{ item.label }}\u003c/Listbox.ItemText\u003e\n        \u003cListbox.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Listbox.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Listbox.Item\u003e\n    \u003c/Listbox.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Listbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Listbox, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/svelte/listbox'\n  import CheckIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/check'\n  import styles from 'styles/listbox.module.css'\n\n  const collection = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { 'fri' },\n      { label: 'Saturday', value: 'sat' },\n      { label: 'Sunday', value: 'sun' },\n    ],\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cListbox.Root class={styles.Root} {collection} selectionMode=\"multiple\"\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSelect Days\u003c/Listbox.Label\u003e\n  \u003cListbox.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n    {#each
